# from tvm.script import ir as I
# from tvm.script import tir as T

@I.ir_module
class Module:
    @T.prim_func
    def main(A: T.Buffer((64, 64), "float32"), B: T.Buffer((64, 64), "float32"), out: T.Buffer((64, 64), "float32")):
        T.func_attr({"from_legacy_te_schedule": T.bool(True), "global_symbol": "main", "tir.noalias": T.bool(True)})
        for i_outer_j_outer_fused in T.parallel(4):
            out_local = T.allocate([1024], "float32", "local")
            out_local_1 = T.Buffer((1024,), data=out_local, scope="local")
            for i_c_outer_outer_inner in range(16):
                out_local_1[i_c_outer_outer_inner * 64:i_c_outer_outer_inner * 64 + 64] = T.Broadcast(T.float32(0), 64)
                for k_outer, k_inner in T.grid(16, 4):
                    cse_var_1: T.int32 = i_c_outer_outer_inner * 64
                    A_1 = T.Buffer((4096,), data=A.data)
                    B_1 = T.Buffer((4096,), data=B.data)
                    out_local_1[cse_var_1:cse_var_1 + 64] = out_local_1[cse_var_1:cse_var_1 + 64] + T.Broadcast(A_1[i_outer_j_outer_fused * 1024 + cse_var_1 + k_outer * 4 + k_inner], 64) * B_1[k_outer * 256 + k_inner * 64:k_outer * 256 + k_inner * 64 + 64]
            for i_inner, j_inner in T.grid(16, 64):
                cse_var_2: T.int32 = i_inner * 64
                out_1 = T.Buffer((4096,), data=out.data)
                out_1[i_outer_j_outer_fused * 1024 + cse_var_2 + j_inner] = out_local_1[cse_var_2 + j_inner]
